3. **Robber Placement Strategy**:
   - The robber is currently on the 🌾9 tile (-1, 2, -1), which is not significantly impacting RED because RED does not have a settlement on this tile.
   - To hinder RED's expansion, we need to place the robber on a tile that RED relies on for resources.

4. **RED's Resource Production**:
   - RED has settlements at nodes 2 and 8.
   - Node 2 produces: 🌾4, 🧱6, 🌲11.
   - Node 8 produces: 🧱6, 🐑5, ⛏️8.
   - RED's critical resources are Brick (🧱6) and Wood (🌲11).

5. **Available Actions**:
   - Moving the robber to (1, -1, 0) will block RED's Brick production (🧱6) at nodes 1 and 2.
   - Moving the robber to (0, -1, 1) will block RED's Wood production (🌲11) at node 2.
   - Both actions will allow BLUE to steal a resource from RED.

6. **Strategic Decision**:
   - Blocking RED's Brick production will hinder their ability to build settlements and cities, which is crucial for their expansion.
   - Blocking RED's Wood production will hinder their ability to build roads and potentially secure the Longest Road bonus.

Given the current plan to hinder RED's expansion and secure the wood port, the best strategic move is to block RED's Wood production.

### Step-by-Step Analysis:

1. **Current Objective**: Secure the wood port and block RED's wood production.
2. **RED's Production**: RED has significant production from the 🌲8 tile at node 10 and the 🌲11 tile at nodes 2 and 10.
3. **Robber Placement**: The robber is currently at (-1, 2, -1), which is not affecting RED's wood production.
4. **Available Actions**:
   - [0] Move robber to (0, 0, 0) and steal from RED
   - [1] Move robber to (1, -1, 0) and steal from RED
   - [2] Move robber to (0, -1, 1) and steal from RED
   - [3] Move robber to (-1, 0, 1)
   - [4] Move robber to (-1, 1, 0)
   - [5] Move robber to (0, 1, -1)
   - [6] Move robber to (1, 0, -1) and steal from RED
   - [7] Move robber to (2, -2, 0) and steal from RED
   - [8] Move robber to (1, -2, 1) and steal from RED
   - [9] Move robber to (0, -2, 2) and steal from RED
   - [10] Move robber to (-1, -1, 2)
   - [11] Move robber to (-2, 0, 2)
   - [12] Move robber to (-2, 1, 1)
   - [13] Move robber to (-2, 2, 0)
   - [14] Move robber to (0, 2, -2)
   - [15] Move robber to (1, 1, -2)
   - [16] Move robber to (2, 0, -2)
   - [17] Move robber to (2, -1, -1) and steal from RED

### Strategic Considerations:

1. **Blocking RED's Wood Production**:
   - The 🌲8 tile at (0, -2, 2) is a critical wood source for RED.
   - Moving the robber to (0, -2, 2) will block RED's wood production from this tile.

2. **Stealing from RED**:
   - Moving the robber to (0, -2, 2) will also allow BLUE to steal a resource from RED, further hindering RED's progress.

3. **Future Turns**:
   - Blocking RED's wood production will slow down their expansion and potentially their ability to build more roads or settlements.
   - This will give BLUE more time to build roads towards the wood port and secure it.

### Conclusion:

Based on the analysis, the best action is to move the robber to (0, -2, 2) to block RED's wood production and steal a resource from RED. This aligns with the current plan to secure the wood port and hinder RED's expansion.

   - BLUE has 2 settlements and 2 roads.

   - BLUE has access to the 2:1 🌲 WOOD port.
   - Other ports are available, but not directly accessible without building more roads.

1. **End Turn**:
   - [0] End your turn

2. **Maritime Trade Options**:
   - [1] Trade port: Give 4 🐑SHEEP for 1 🌲WOOD
   - [2] Trade port: Give 4 🐑SHEEP for 1 🧱BRICK
   - [3] Trade port: Give 4 🐑SHEEP for 1 ⛏️ORE
   - [4] Trade port: Give 4 🐑SHEEP for 1 🌾WHEAT

### Decision Making:
1. **Resource Analysis**:
   - BLUE has a surplus of 🐑SHEEP (4 cards).
   - BLUE needs more 🌲WOOD to build roads and expand.

2. **Immediate Needs**:
   - To continue the plan of building roads towards the wood port and securing it, BLUE needs more 🌲WOOD.
   - Trading 4 🐑SHEEP for 1 🌲WOOD is a good move to accelerate road building.

3. **Future Turns**:
   - With more 🌲WOOD, BLUE can build roads and potentially secure the wood port, which will be beneficial for future trades.
   - Building roads will also help in blocking RED's wood production, hindering their expansion.

### Conclusion:
Given the current resources and the strategic plan, the best action is to trade 4 🐑SHEEP for 1 🌲WOOD to continue building roads towards the wood port.
